SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
/****** Script for SelectTopNRows command from SSMS  ******/
CREATE PROC [dbo].[spGET_FUND_SCRIP_BUCKET_SYMBOL_EXIST]
	@Symbol varchar(MAX)
AS
BEGIN
DECLARE @Data varchar(MAX)
	SELECT @Data = [FSB_SHARE_SYMBOL] FROM [FUND_SCRIP_BUCKET]
	WHERE [FSB_SHARE_SYMBOL] = @Symbol
	IF @Data IS NULL 
		BEGIN
			SELECT 'Nil'
		END
	ELSE
		BEGIN
			SELECT @Data
		END
	
END
GO

/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[spGET_SCRIP_SYMBOL_FROM_SCRIP_NAME]    Script Date: 12/2/2020 5:44:35 PM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE PROC [dbo].[spGET_SCRIP_SYMBOL_FROM_SCRIP_NAME]
		@CompanyName varchar(MAX)
		AS
		BEGIN
		DECLARE @value varchar(MAX)
			SELECT @value = SI_SYMBOL FROM SCRIP_INFO WHERE SI_NAME = REPLACE(REPLACE(REPLACE(REPLACE(REPLACE(REPLACE(@CompanyName,'(XD)',''),'(XR)',''),'(XB)',''),'(XDXB)',''),' [ DEFAULTER SEGMENT ]',''),'(R)','')
			IF @value is null
				BEGIN
					IF  @CompanyName like '%-JAN' OR @CompanyName like '%-FEB' OR @CompanyName like '%-MAR' OR @CompanyName like '%-APR' OR @CompanyName like '%-MAY' OR @CompanyName like '%-JUN' OR @CompanyName like '%-JUL' OR @CompanyName like '%-AUG' OR @CompanyName like '%-SEP' OR @CompanyName like '%-OCT' OR @CompanyName like '%-NOV' OR @CompanyName like '%-DEC'
						BEGIN
							SELECT REPLACE(REPLACE(REPLACE(REPLACE(REPLACE(REPLACE(REPLACE(REPLACE(REPLACE(REPLACE(REPLACE(REPLACE(@CompanyName,'-OCT',''),'-NOV',''),'-DEC',''),'-JAN',''),'-FEB',''),'-MAR',''),'-APR',''),'-MAY',''),'-JUN',''),'-JUL',''),'AUG',''),'SEP','') AS C_SYMBOL
						END
					ELSE
						BEGIN
							SELECT 'Nil' AS C_SYMBOL
						END
				END
			ELSE
				BEGIN
					SELECT @value AS C_SYMBOL
				END
		END
GO

/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[spGetShareDetailByParamFundIdAndDate]    Script Date: 12/2/2020 5:44:35 PM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO

CREATE PROC [dbo].[spGetShareDetailByParamFundIdAndDate]
		@FUND_ID int,
		@DATE date
AS
BEGIN

select share_name, share_symbol,  
(select Top 1 (movAvg_tranDate)  from pms_movingAvg
where pms_movingAvg.tradInstType_code=1 and pms_movingAvg.tradInst_code = share_code and pms_movingAvg.fund_code=@FUND_ID and movAvg_tranDate<@DATE 

) as DateCostLastUpdated,

(select Top 1 movAvg_average from pms_movingAvg
where pms_movingAvg.tradInstType_code=1 and pms_movingAvg.tradInst_code = share_code and pms_movingAvg.fund_code=@FUND_ID
and movAvg_tranDate = (select max(movAvg_tranDate)  from pms_movingAvg
where pms_movingAvg.tradInstType_code=1 and pms_movingAvg.tradInst_code = share_code and pms_movingAvg.fund_code=@FUND_ID and movAvg_tranDate<@DATE)
order by movAvg_tranDate desc) as LastUpdatedPerUnitCost,


(select Top 1 movAvg_amtMov from pms_movingAvg
where pms_movingAvg.tradInstType_code=1 and pms_movingAvg.tradInst_code = share_code and pms_movingAvg.fund_code=@FUND_ID
and movAvg_tranDate = (select max(movAvg_tranDate)  from pms_movingAvg
where pms_movingAvg.tradInstType_code=1 and pms_movingAvg.tradInst_code = share_code and pms_movingAvg.fund_code=@FUND_ID and movAvg_tranDate<@DATE)
order by movAvg_tranDate desc) as LastUpdatedCost,

(select Top 1 movAvg_qty from pms_movingAvg
where pms_movingAvg.tradInstType_code=1 and pms_movingAvg.tradInst_code = share_code and pms_movingAvg.fund_code=@FUND_ID
and movAvg_tranDate = (select max(movAvg_tranDate)  from pms_movingAvg
where pms_movingAvg.tradInstType_code=1 and pms_movingAvg.tradInst_code = share_code and pms_movingAvg.fund_code=@FUND_ID and movAvg_tranDate<@DATE)
order by movAvg_tranDate desc) as LastUpdatedHolding,

(select 1) as LastUpdatedMarketPriceDate

from pms_shares

END
GO

CREATE PROC [dbo].[spGetSymbolFromCompanyName]
		@CompanyName varchar(500)
		AS
		BEGIN
		DECLARE @value varchar(500)
			SELECT @value = SI_SYMBOL FROM SCRIP_INFO WHERE SI_NAME = REPLACE(REPLACE(REPLACE(REPLACE(REPLACE(REPLACE(@CompanyName,'(XD)',''),'(XR)',''),'(XB)',''),'(XDXB)',''),' [ DEFAULTER SEGMENT ]',''),'(R)','')
			IF @value is null
				BEGIN
					IF  @CompanyName like '%-JAN' OR @CompanyName like '%-FEB' OR @CompanyName like '%-MAR' OR @CompanyName like '%-APR' OR @CompanyName like '%-MAY' OR @CompanyName like '%-JUN' OR @CompanyName like '%-JUL' OR @CompanyName like '%-AUG' OR @CompanyName like '%-SEP' OR @CompanyName like '%-OCT' OR @CompanyName like '%-NOV' OR @CompanyName like '%-DEC'
						BEGIN
							SELECT REPLACE(REPLACE(REPLACE(REPLACE(REPLACE(REPLACE(REPLACE(REPLACE(REPLACE(REPLACE(REPLACE(REPLACE(@CompanyName,'-OCT',''),'-NOV',''),'-DEC',''),'-JAN',''),'-FEB',''),'-MAR',''),'-APR',''),'-MAY',''),'-JUN',''),'-JUL',''),'AUG',''),'SEP','') AS C_SYMBOL
						END
					ELSE
						BEGIN
							SELECT 'Nil' AS C_SYMBOL
						END
				END
			ELSE
				BEGIN
					SELECT @value AS C_SYMBOL
				END
		END
GO

CREATE PROC [dbo].[spINSERT_APP_STATUS]
	@APS_TASK_DATE datetime,
	@APS_TABLE varchar(500),
	@APS_STATUS varchar(MAX),
	@APS_CLEARING_TABLE bit,
	@APS_FETCHING_DATA bit,
	@APS_DUMPING_DATA bit,
	@APS_FETCH_DATA_START_TIME datetime,
	@APS_FETCH_DATA_END_TIME datetime,
	@APS_DUMP_DATA_TIME datetime,
	@APS_COMMENTS varchar(MAX)
AS
BEGIN
INSERT INTO [dbo].[APP_STATUS]
           ([APS_TASK_DATE]
		   ,[APS_TABLE]
           ,[APS_STATUS]
           ,[APS_CLEARING_TABLE]
           ,[APS_FETCHING_DATA]
           ,[APS_DUMPING_DATA]
           ,[APS_FETCH_DATA_START_TIME]
           ,[APS_FETCH_DATA_END_TIME]
           ,[APS_DUMP_DATA_TIME]
           ,[APS_COMMENTS])
     VALUES
           (@APS_TASK_DATE
		   ,@APS_TABLE
           ,@APS_STATUS
           ,@APS_CLEARING_TABLE
           ,@APS_FETCHING_DATA
           ,@APS_DUMPING_DATA
           ,@APS_FETCH_DATA_START_TIME
           ,@APS_FETCH_DATA_END_TIME
           ,@APS_DUMP_DATA_TIME
           ,@APS_COMMENTS)
END
GO

           ,@SHR_AVG_PRICE
           ,@SHR_BOOK_COST

           ,@SHR_MARKET_VALUE
           ,@SHR_APP_DEP)

CREATE PROC [dbo].[spINSERT_FUND_SCRIP_BUCKET]
	@FSB_DATE Datetime,
	@FSB_STATUS varchar(max),
	@FSB_READING_STATUS bit,
	@FSB_FUND_ID bigint,
	@FSB_FUND_NAME varchar(max),
	@FSB_SHARE_NAME varchar(max),
	@FSB_SHARE_SYMBOL varchar(500),
	@FSB_SHARE_QUANTITY decimal(18,2),
	@FSB_SHARE_AVG_PRICE decimal(18,2),
	@FSB_SHARE_BOOK_COST decimal(18,2),
	@FSB_SHARE_MARKET_PRICE decimal(18,2),
	@FSB_SHARE_MARKET_VALUE decimal(18,2),
	@FSB_SHARE_APP_DEP decimal(18,2),
	@FSB_SHARE_PERCENTAGE_CLOSING decimal(18,2)
AS
BEGIN
	INSERT INTO [dbo].[FUND_SCRIP_BUCKET]
           ([FSB_DATE]
           ,[FSB_STATUS]
	       ,[FSB_READING_STATUS]
           ,[FSB_FUND_ID]
           ,[FSB_FUND_NAME]
           ,[FSB_SHARE_NAME]
           ,[FSB_SHARE_SYMBOL]
           ,[FSB_SHARE_QUANTITY]
           ,[FSB_SHARE_AVG_PRICE]
           ,[FSB_SHARE_BOOK_COST]
           ,[FSB_SHARE_MARKET_PRICE]
           ,[FSB_SHARE_MARKET_VALUE]
           ,[FSB_SHARE_APP_DEP]
           ,[FSB_SHARE_PERCENTAGE_CLOSING])
     VALUES
           (@FSB_DATE
           ,@FSB_STATUS
	       ,@FSB_READING_STATUS
           ,@FSB_FUND_ID
           ,@FSB_FUND_NAME
           ,@FSB_SHARE_NAME
           ,@FSB_SHARE_SYMBOL
           ,@FSB_SHARE_QUANTITY
           ,@FSB_SHARE_AVG_PRICE
           ,@FSB_SHARE_BOOK_COST
           ,@FSB_SHARE_MARKET_PRICE
           ,@FSB_SHARE_MARKET_VALUE
           ,@FSB_SHARE_APP_DEP
           ,@FSB_SHARE_PERCENTAGE_CLOSING)

CREATE PROC [dbo].[spInsertMarketSummary] 
		@COMPANY_NAME varchar(MAX),
		@COMPANY_SYMBOL varchar(MAX),
		@COMPANY_LDCP float,
		@COMPANY_OPEN float,
		@COMPANY_HIGH float,
		@COMPANY_LOW float,
		@COMPANY_CURRENT float,
		@COMPANY_CHANGE float,
		@COMPANY_VOLUME float
	AS
BEGIN

INSERT INTO [dbo].[CURRENT_MARKET_SUMMARY]
           ([CMS_SECTOR]
		   ,[CMS_SCRIP_NAME]
           ,[CMS_SYMBOL]
           ,[CMS_LDCP]
           ,[CMS_OPEN]
           ,[CMS_HIGH]
           ,[CMS_LOW]
           ,[CMS_CURRENT]
           ,[CMS_CHANGE]
           ,[CMS_VOLUME])
     VALUES
           (''
		   ,UPPER(@COMPANY_NAME)
           ,UPPER(@COMPANY_SYMBOL)
           ,@COMPANY_LDCP
           ,@COMPANY_OPEN
           ,@COMPANY_HIGH 
           ,@COMPANY_LOW
           ,@COMPANY_CURRENT
           ,@COMPANY_CHANGE
           ,@COMPANY_VOLUME)
END
GO

CREATE PROC [dbo].[spIsGetCompanySymbolExist]
		@SYMBOL varchar(500)
		AS
BEGIN
	DECLARE @Count bigint;
	SELECT @Count = COUNT(*) FROM [SCRIP_INFO] WHERE [SI_SYMBOL] = @SYMBOL 
	SELECT @Count AS [FUND_EXIST]
END

CREATE PROC [dbo].[spUPDATE_APP_STATUS]
	@ID int,
	@APS_TASK_DATE datetime,
	@APS_TABLE varchar(500),
	@APS_STATUS varchar(MAX),
	@APS_CLEARING_TABLE bit,
	@APS_FETCHING_DATA bit,
	@APS_DUMPING_DATA bit,
	@APS_FETCH_DATA_START_TIME datetime,
	@APS_FETCH_DATA_END_TIME datetime,
	@APS_DUMP_DATA_TIME datetime,
	@APS_COMMENTS varchar(MAX)
AS
BEGIN

UPDATE [dbo].[APP_STATUS]
   SET [APS_TASK_DATE] = @APS_TASK_DATE
      ,[APS_TABLE] = @APS_TABLE
      ,[APS_STATUS] = @APS_STATUS
      ,[APS_CLEARING_TABLE] = @APS_CLEARING_TABLE
      ,[APS_FETCHING_DATA] = @APS_FETCHING_DATA
      ,[APS_DUMPING_DATA] = @APS_DUMPING_DATA
      ,[APS_FETCH_DATA_START_TIME] = @APS_FETCH_DATA_START_TIME
      ,[APS_FETCH_DATA_END_TIME] = @APS_FETCH_DATA_END_TIME
      ,[APS_DUMP_DATA_TIME] = @APS_DUMP_DATA_TIME
      ,[APS_COMMENTS] = @APS_COMMENTS
 WHERE APS_ID = 1

END
GO

CREATE PROC [dbo].[spUPDATE_FUND_SCRIP_BUCKET]
	@FSB_DATE Datetime,
	@FSB_STATUS varchar(max),
	@FSB_FUND_ID bigint,
	@FSB_FUND_NAME varchar(max),
	@FSB_SHARE_NAME varchar(max),
	@FSB_SHARE_SYMBOL varchar(500),
	@FSB_SHARE_QUANTITY decimal(18,2),
	@FSB_SHARE_AVG_PRICE decimal(18,2),
	@FSB_SHARE_BOOK_COST decimal(18,2),
	@FSB_SHARE_MARKET_PRICE decimal(18,2),
	@FSB_SHARE_MARKET_VALUE decimal(18,2),
	@FSB_SHARE_APP_DEP decimal(18,2),
	@FSB_SHARE_PERCENTAGE_CLOSING decimal(18,2)
AS
BEGIN
UPDATE [dbo].[FUND_SCRIP_BUCKET]
   SET [FSB_DATE] = @FSB_DATE
      ,[FSB_STATUS] = @FSB_STATUS
      ,[FSB_FUND_ID] = @FSB_FUND_ID
      ,[FSB_FUND_NAME] = @FSB_FUND_NAME
      ,[FSB_SHARE_NAME] = @FSB_SHARE_NAME
      ,[FSB_SHARE_SYMBOL] = @FSB_SHARE_SYMBOL
      ,[FSB_SHARE_QUANTITY] = @FSB_SHARE_QUANTITY
      ,[FSB_SHARE_AVG_PRICE] = @FSB_SHARE_AVG_PRICE
      ,[FSB_SHARE_BOOK_COST] = @FSB_SHARE_BOOK_COST
      ,[FSB_SHARE_MARKET_PRICE] = @FSB_SHARE_MARKET_PRICE
      ,[FSB_SHARE_MARKET_VALUE] = @FSB_SHARE_MARKET_VALUE
      ,[FSB_SHARE_APP_DEP] = @FSB_SHARE_APP_DEP
      ,[FSB_SHARE_PERCENTAGE_CLOSING] = @FSB_SHARE_PERCENTAGE_CLOSING
 WHERE [FSB_SHARE_SYMBOL] = @FSB_SHARE_SYMBOL
END

CREATE PROC [dbo].[spUpdateMarketSummary] 
		@COMPANY_NAME varchar(300),
		@COMPANY_SYMBOL varchar(300),
		@COMPANY_LDCP float,
		@COMPANY_OPEN float,
		@COMPANY_HIGH float,
		@COMPANY_LOW float,
		@COMPANY_CURRENT float,
		@COMPANY_CHANGE float,
		@COMPANY_VOLUME float
	AS

   SET
      [MS_COMPANY_SYMBOL] = @COMPANY_SYMBOL
      ,[MS_COMPANY_LDCP] = @COMPANY_LDCP
      ,[MS_COMPANY_OPEN] = @COMPANY_OPEN
      ,[MS_COMPANY_HIGH] = @COMPANY_HIGH
      ,[MS_COMPANY_LOW] = @COMPANY_LOW 
      ,[MS_COMPANY_CURRENT] = @COMPANY_CURRENT
      ,[MS_COMPANY_CHANGE] = @COMPANY_CHANGE
      ,[MS_COMPANY_VOLUME] = @COMPANY_VOLUME
 WHERE [MS_COMPANY_NAME] = @COMPANY_NAME
END

CREATE PROC [dbo].[spUpdateMarketSummaryOverview]
		@DATE DATETIME,
		@STATUS varchar(300),
		@VOLUME float,
		@VALUE float,
		@TRADES float
		AS
		BEGIN
UPDATE [dbo].[MarketSummaryOverview]
   SET [MS_DATE] = @DATE
      ,[MS_STATUS] = @STATUS
      ,[MS_VOLUME] = @VOLUME
      ,[MS_VALUE] = @VALUE
      ,[MS_TRADES] = @TRADES
 WHERE MS_ID = 1
END
